# <a name="com-error-codes-comadmin-filter-graphics"></a><span data-ttu-id="88742-104">COM 錯誤碼 (COMADMIN、篩選、圖形) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-104">COM Error Codes (COMADMIN, FILTER, GRAPHICS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="88742-105">下表提供以 COM 為基礎的 Api 所使用的錯誤碼清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-105">The following table provides a list of error codes used by COM-based APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="88742-106">如果您在安裝或執行的應用程式遇到困難，請洽詢客戶對顯示錯誤訊息之軟體的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-106">If you are experiencing difficulty with an application you are installing or running, contact customer support for the software that is displaying the error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="88742-107">若要取得 Microsoft 產品的支援，請移至 [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-107">To obtain support for a Microsoft product, go to [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go).</span></span>

| <span id="COMADMIN_E_OBJECTERRORS"></span><span id="comadmin_e_objecterrors"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-110"><dt>**COMADMIN \_E \_ OBJECTERRORS**</dt> <dt>0x80110401</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-110"><dt>**COMADMIN\_E\_OBJECTERRORS**</dt> <dt>0x80110401</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                                                  | <span data-ttu-id="88742-111">存取一或多個物件時發生錯誤-ErrorInfo 集合可能有更多詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-111">Errors occurred accessing one or more objects - the ErrorInfo collection may have more detail</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |

| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_MIRRORING_DEVICES_NOT_SUPPORTED"></span><span id="error_graphics_mirroring_devices_not_supported"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-841"><dt>**錯誤 \_\_ \_ \_ 不 \_ 支援的圖形鏡像裝置**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E3</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-841"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_MIRRORING\_DEVICES\_NOT\_SUPPORTED**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E3</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                          | <span data-ttu-id="88742-842">此函數不支援 GDI 鏡像顯示裝置，因為 GDI 鏡像顯示裝置沒有任何相關聯的實體監視器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-842">This function does not support GDI mirroring display devices because GDI mirroring display devices do not have any physical monitors associated with them.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_INVALID_POINTER"></span><span id="error_graphics_invalid_pointer"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-843"><dt>**錯誤 \_圖形 \_ 不正確 \_ 指標**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E4</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-843"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_INVALID\_POINTER**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E4</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                            | <span data-ttu-id="88742-844">因為傳遞了不正確指標參數，所以函式失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-844">The function failed because an invalid pointer parameter was passed to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="88742-845">如果指標參數為 **Null**、指向不正確位址、指向核心模式位址，或未正確對齊，則為不正確指標參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-845">A pointer parameter is invalid if it is **NULL**, points to an invalid address, points to a kernel mode address, or is not correctly aligned.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_NO_MONITORS_CORRESPOND_TO_DISPLAY_DEVICE"></span><span id="error_graphics_no_monitors_correspond_to_display_device"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-846"><dt>**錯誤 \_圖形 \_ 沒有任何 \_ 監視器 \_ 對應 \_ 到 \_ 顯示 \_ 設備**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E5</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-846"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_NO\_MONITORS\_CORRESPOND\_TO\_DISPLAY\_DEVICE**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E5</dt></span></span> </dl>                                             | <span data-ttu-id="88742-847">函數失敗，因為指定的 GDI 裝置沒有任何與其相關聯的監視器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-847">The function failed because the specified GDI device did not have any monitors associated with it.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_PARAMETER_ARRAY_TOO_SMALL"></span><span id="error_graphics_parameter_array_too_small"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-848"><dt>**錯誤 \_圖形 \_ 參數 \_ 陣列 \_ 太 \_ 小**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E6</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-848"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_PARAMETER\_ARRAY\_TOO\_SMALL**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E6</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                            | <span data-ttu-id="88742-849">傳遞至函式的陣列不能保存函式必須複製到陣列中的所有資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-849">An array passed to the function cannot hold all of the data that the function must copy into the array.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_INTERNAL_ERROR"></span><span id="error_graphics_internal_error"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-850"><dt>**錯誤 \_圖形 \_ 內部 \_ 錯誤**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E7</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-850"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_INTERNAL\_ERROR**</dt> <dt>0xC02625E7</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                               | <span data-ttu-id="88742-851">發生內部錯誤，導致作業失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-851">An internal error caused an operation to fail.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_SESSION_TYPE_CHANGE_IN_PROGRESS"></span><span id="error_graphics_session_type_change_in_progress"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="88742-852"><dt>**錯誤 \_\_ \_ \_ \_ \_ 正在進行圖形會話類型變更**</dt> <dt>0xC02605E8</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-852"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_SESSION\_TYPE\_CHANGE\_IN\_PROGRESS**</dt> <dt>0xC02605E8</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                         | <span data-ttu-id="88742-853">函數失敗，因為目前的會話正在變更其類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-853">The function failed because the current session is changing its type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="88742-854">當目前的會話正在變更其類型時，無法呼叫此函數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-854">This function cannot be called when the current session is changing its type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="88742-855">目前有三種類型的會話：主控台、已中斷連線及遠端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88742-855">There are currently three types of sessions: console, disconnected and remote.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
